(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing that its Board of Directors approved a 7.5% increase in its annualized dividend rate to $0.86 per share, from the current annualized rate of $0.80 per share, effective with the regular quarterly cash dividend announced on the same day.
